<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-right: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">8.4 &#22312;&#36829;&#32422;&#26102;&#65292;&#26681;&#25454;&#20013;&#22269;&#26377;&#20851;&#27861;&#24459;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#26377;&#26435;&#25353;&#29031;&#27861;&#23450;&#31243;&#24207;&#22788;&#32622;&#36136;&#25276;&#32929;&#26435;&#12290;&#22312;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#20801;&#35768;&#30340;&#33539;&#22260;&#20869;&#65292;&#23545;&#20110;&#22788;&#32622;&#30340;&#25152;&#24471;&#65292;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#26080;&#38656;&#32473;&#20184;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#65307;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#29305;&#27492;&#25918;&#24323;&#20854;&#21487;&#33021;&#26377;&#30340;&#33021;&#21521;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#35201;&#27714;&#20219;&#20309;&#36136;&#25276;&#32929;&#26435;&#22788;&#32622;&#25152;&#24471;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">In the event of default, Pledgee is entitled
to dispose of the Equity Interest in accordance with applicable PRC laws. Only to the extent permitted under applicable PRC laws, Pledgee
has no obligation to account to Pledger for proceeds of disposition of the Equity Interest, and Pledger hereby waives any rights it may
have to demand any such accounting from Pledgee.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">8.5 &#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#20381;&#29031;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#22788;&#20998;&#36136;&#26435;&#26102;&#65292;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#24212;&#20104;&#20197;&#24517;&#35201;&#30340;&#21327;&#21161;&#65292;&#20197;&#20351;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#23454;&#29616;&#20854;&#36136;&#26435;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">When Pledgee disposes of the Pledge in
accordance with this Agreement, Pledger and Party C shall provide necessary assistance to enable Pledgee to enforce the Pledge in accordance
with this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>9. &#36716;&#35753;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"><B>Assignment</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.1 &#38500;&#38750;&#32463;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#20107;&#20808;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#26080;&#26435;&#36192;&#20104;&#25110;&#36716;&#35753;&#20854;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#20041;&#21153;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">Without Pledgee's prior written consent,
Pledger shall not have the right to assign or delegate its rights and obligations under this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.2 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#23545;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#21450;&#20854;&#32487;&#20219;&#20154;&#21644;&#32463;&#35768;&#21487;&#30340;&#21463;&#35753;&#20154;&#22343;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#65292;&#24182;&#19988;&#23545;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#21450;&#27599;&#19968;&#32487;&#20219;&#20154;&#21644;&#21463;&#35753;&#20154;&#26377;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">This Agreement shall be binding on Pledger
and its successors and permitted assigns, and shall be valid with respect to Pledgee and each of its successors and assigns.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.3 &#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#21487;&#20197;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26102;&#20505;&#23558;&#20854;&#22312;&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#26435;&#21033;&#21644;&#20041;&#21153;&#36716;&#35753;&#32473;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20154;&#65288;&#33258;&#28982;&#20154;/&#27861;&#20154;&#65289;&#65292;&#22312;&#36825;&#31181;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;&#65292;&#21463;&#35753;&#20154;&#24212;&#20139;&#26377;&#21644;&#25215;&#25285;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#20139;&#26377;&#21644;&#25215;&#25285;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#21644;&#20041;&#21153;&#65292;&#22914;&#21516;&#20854;&#20316;&#20026;&#21407;&#21512;&#21516;&#26041;&#24212;&#20139;&#26377;&#21644;&#25215;&#25285;&#30340;&#19968;&#26679;&#12290;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#36716;&#35753;&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#21644;&#20041;&#21153;&#26102;&#65292;&#24212;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#24212;&#23601;&#27492;&#36716;&#35753;&#31614;&#32626;&#26377;&#20851;&#21327;&#35758;&#21644;/&#25110;&#25991;&#20214;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">At any time, Pledgee may assign any and
all of its rights and obligations under the Control Agreements to its designee(s) (natural/legal persons), in which case the assigns shall
have the rights and obligations of Pledgee under this Agreement, as if it were the original party to this Agreement. When the Pledgee
assigns the rights and obligations under the Control Agreements, upon Pledgee's request, Pledger shall execute relevant agreements or
other documents relating to such assignment.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.4 &#22240;&#36716;&#35753;&#25152;&#23548;&#33268;&#30340;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#21464;&#26356;&#21518;&#65292;&#24212;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#24212;&#19982;&#26032;&#30340;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#31614;&#35746;&#19968;&#20221;&#20869;&#23481;&#19982;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#19968;&#33268;&#30340;&#26032;&#36136;&#25276;&#21512;&#21516;&#65292;&#24182;&#22312;&#30456;&#24212;&#30340;&#24037;&#21830;&#34892;&#25919;&#31649;&#29702;&#26426;&#20851;&#36827;&#34892;&#30331;&#35760;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">In the event of a change in Pledgee due
to an assignment, Pledger shall, at the request of Pledgee, execute a new pledge agreement with the new pledgee on the same terms and
conditions as this Agreement, and register the same with the relevant AIC.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.5 &#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#24212;&#20005;&#26684;&#36981;&#23432;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#21508;&#26041;&#21333;&#29420;&#25110;&#20849;&#21516;&#31614;&#32626;&#30340;&#20854;&#20182;&#26377;&#20851;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#21253;&#25324;&#32929;&#26435;&#22788;&#20998;&#21512;&#21516;&#21644;&#23545;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#30340;&#25480;&#26435;&#22996;&#25176;&#20070;&#65292;&#23653;&#34892;&#21508;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20041;&#21153;&#65292;&#24182;&#19981;&#24471;&#36827;&#34892;&#20219;&#20309;&#36275;&#20197;&#24433;&#21709;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#26377;&#25928;&#24615;&#21644;&#21487;&#24378;&#21046;&#25191;&#34892;&#24615;&#30340;&#20316;&#20026;/&#19981;&#20316;&#20026;&#34892;&#20026;&#12290;&#38500;&#38750;&#26681;&#25454;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#30340;&#20070;&#38754;&#25351;&#31034;&#65292;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#19981;&#24471;&#34892;&#20351;&#20854;&#23545;&#36136;&#25276;&#32929;&#26435;&#36824;&#30041;&#23384;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">Pledger shall strictly abide by the provisions
of this Agreement and other contracts jointly or separately executed by the Parties hereto or any of them, including the Equity Option
Agreement and the Power of Attorney granted to Pledgee, perform the obligations hereunder and thereunder, and refrain from any action/omission
that may affect the effectiveness and enforceability thereof. Any remaining rights of Pledger with respect to the Equity Interest pledged
hereunder shall not be exercised by Pledger except in accordance with the written instructions of Pledgee.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>10. &#32456;&#27490;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"><B>Termination</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&#22312;&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#21672;&#35810;&#26381;&#21153;&#36153;&#31561;&#36153;&#29992;&#20607;&#36824;&#23436;&#27605;&#65292;&#24182;&#19988;&#19993;&#26041;&#19981;&#20877;&#25215;&#25285;&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20041;&#21153;&#20043;&#21518;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32456;&#27490;&#65292;&#24182;&#19988;&#22312;&#23613;&#26089;&#21512;&#29702;&#21487;&#34892;&#30340;&#26102;&#38388;&#20869;&#65292;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#24212;&#35299;&#38500;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#19979;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#36136;&#25276;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">Upon the full payment of the consulting
and service fees under the Control Agreements and upon termination of Party C's obligations under the Control Agreements, this Agreement
shall be terminated, and Pledgee shall then terminate the equity pledge under this Agreement as soon as reasonably practicable.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>11. &#25163;&#32493;&#36153;&#21450;&#20854;&#20182;&#36153;&#29992;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 2.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.1pt"><B>Handling Fees
and Other Expenses</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 2.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&#19968;&#20999;&#19982;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#36153;&#29992;&#21450;&#23454;&#38469;&#24320;&#25903;&#65292;&#20854;&#20013;&#21253;&#25324;&#20294;&#19981;&#38480;&#20110;&#27861;&#24459;&#36153;&#29992;&#12289;&#24037;&#26412;&#36153;&#12289;&#21360;&#33457;&#31246;&#20197;&#21450;&#20219;&#20309;&#20854;&#20182;&#31246;&#25910;&#12289;&#36153;&#29992;&#31561;&#20840;&#37096;&#30001;&#19993;&#26041;&#25215;&#25285;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">All fees and out of pocket expenses relating
to this Agreement, including but not limited to legal costs, costs of production, stamp tax and any other taxes and fees, shall be borne
by Party C.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>12. &#20445;&#23494;&#36131;&#20219;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"><B>Confidentiality</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&#21508;&#26041;&#25215;&#35748;&#21450;&#30830;&#23450;&#26377;&#20851;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#12289;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20869;&#23481;&#65292;&#20197;&#21450;&#24444;&#27492;&#23601;&#20934;&#22791;&#25110;&#23653;&#34892;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#20132;&#25442;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#21475;&#22836;&#25110;&#20070;&#38754;&#36164;&#26009;&#22343;&#34987;&#35270;&#20026;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#12290;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#24403;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#35813;&#31561;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#20104;&#20197;&#20445;&#23494;&#65292;&#32780;&#22312;&#26410;&#24471;&#21040;&#21478;&#19968;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#21069;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#31532;&#19977;&#32773;&#25259;&#38706;&#20219;&#20309;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#65292;&#24799;&#19979;&#21015;&#20449;&#24687;&#38500;&#22806;&#65306;(a)&#20844;&#20247;&#20154;&#22763;&#30693;&#24713;&#25110;&#23558;&#20250;&#30693;&#24713;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20449;&#24687;&#65288;&#24799;&#24182;&#38750;&#30001;&#25509;&#21463;&#20445;&#23494;&#20449;&#24687;&#20043;&#19968;&#26041;&#25797;&#33258;&#21521;&#20844;&#20247;&#25259;&#38706;&#65289;&#65307;(b)&#26681;&#25454;&#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;&#27861;&#35268;&#12289;&#32929;&#31080;&#20132;&#26131;&#35268;&#21017;&#12289;&#25110;&#25919;&#24220;&#37096;&#38376;&#25110;&#27861;&#38498;&#30340;&#21629;&#20196;&#32780;&#25152;&#38656;&#25259;&#38706;&#20043;&#20219;&#20309;&#20449;&#24687;&#65307;&#25110;(c)&#30001;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#23601;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25152;&#36848;&#20132;&#26131;&#32780;&#38656;&#21521;&#20854;&#32929;&#19996;&#12289;&#25237;&#36164;&#32773;&#12289;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#36130;&#21153;&#39038;&#38382;&#25259;&#38706;&#20043;&#20449;&#24687;&#65292;&#32780;&#35813;&#32929;&#19996;&#12289;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#36130;&#21153;&#39038;&#38382;&#20134;&#38656;&#36981;&#23432;&#19982;&#26412;&#26465;&#27454;&#30456;&#31867;&#20284;&#20043;&#20445;&#23494;&#36131;&#20219;&#12290;&#22914;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#24037;&#20316;&#20154;&#21592;&#25110;&#32856;&#35831;&#26426;&#26500;&#30340;&#27844;&#23494;&#22343;&#35270;&#20026;&#35813;&#26041;&#30340;&#27844;&#23494;&#65292;&#38656;&#20381;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25215;&#25285;&#36829;&#32422;&#36131;&#20219;&#12290;&#26080;&#35770;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#29702;&#30001;&#32456;&#27490;&#65292;&#26412;&#26465;&#27454;&#20173;&#28982;&#29983;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">The Parties acknowledge that the existence
and the terms of this Agreement and any oral or written information exchanged between the Parties in connection with the preparation and
performance this Agreement are regarded as confidential information. Each Party shall maintain confidentiality of all such confidential
information, and without obtaining the written consent of the other Party, it shall not disclose any relevant confidential information
to any third parties, except for the information that: (a) is or will be in the public domain (other than through the receiving Party&rsquo;s
unauthorized disclosure); (b) is under the obligation to be disclosed pursuant to the applicable laws or regulations, rules of any stock
exchange, or orders of the court or other government authorities; or (c) is required to be disclosed by any Party to its shareholders,
investors, legal counsels or financial advisors regarding the transaction contemplated hereunder, provided that such shareholders, investors,
legal counsels or financial advisors shall be bound by the confidentiality obligations similar to those set forth in this Section. Disclosure
of any confidential information by the staff members or agencies hired by any Party shall be deemed disclosure of such confidential information
by such Party, which Party shall be held liable for breach of this Agreement. This Section shall survive the termination of this Agreement
for any reason.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>13. &#36866;&#29992;&#27861;&#24459;&#21644;&#20105;&#35758;&#30340;&#35299;&#20915;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"><B>Governing Law and Resolution
of Disputes</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">13.1 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#35746;&#31435;&#12289;&#25928;&#21147;&#12289;&#35299;&#37322;&#12289;&#23653;&#34892;&#12289;&#20462;&#25913;&#21644;&#32456;&#27490;&#20197;&#21450;&#20105;&#35758;&#30340;&#35299;&#20915;&#22343;&#36866;&#29992;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">The execution, effectiveness, construction,
performance, amendment and termination of this Agreement and the resolution of disputes hereunder shall be governed by the laws of China.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">13.2 &#22240;&#35299;&#37322;&#21644;&#23653;&#34892;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#39318;&#20808;&#36890;&#36807;&#21451;&#22909;&#21327;&#21830;&#30340;&#26041;&#24335;&#21152;&#20197;&#35299;&#20915;&#12290;&#22914;&#26524;&#22312;&#19968;&#26041;&#21521;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#21457;&#20986;&#35201;&#27714;&#21327;&#21830;&#35299;&#20915;&#30340;&#20070;&#38754;&#36890;&#30693;&#21518;30&#22825;&#20043;&#20869;&#20105;&#35758;&#20173;&#28982;&#24471;&#19981;&#21040;&#35299;&#20915;&#65292;&#21017;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#22343;&#21487;&#23558;&#26377;&#20851;&#20105;&#35758;&#25552;&#20132;&#32473;&#20301;&#20110;&#28145;&#22323;&#30340;&#20013;&#22269;&#22269;&#38469;&#32463;&#27982;&#36152;&#26131;&#20210;&#35009;&#22996;&#21592;&#20250;&#21326;&#21335;&#20998;&#20250;&#65292;&#30001;&#35813;&#20250;&#25353;&#29031;&#20013;&#22269;&#22269;&#38469;&#32463;&#27982;&#36152;&#26131;&#20210;&#35009;&#22996;&#21592;&#20250;&#20210;&#35009;&#35268;&#21017;&#20210;&#35009;&#35299;&#20915;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#24212;&#22312;&#28145;&#22323;&#36827;&#34892;&#65292;&#20351;&#29992;&#20043;&#35821;&#35328;&#20026;&#20013;&#25991;&#12290;&#20210;&#35009;&#35009;&#20915;&#26159;&#32456;&#23616;&#24615;&#30340;&#65292;&#23545;&#21508;&#26041;&#22343;&#26377;&#32422;&#26463;&#21147;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">In the event of any dispute with respect
to the construction and performance of this Agreement, the Parties shall first resolve the dispute through friendly negotiations. In the
event the Parties fail to reach an agreement on the dispute within 30 days after either Party's request to the other Parties for resolution
of the dispute through negotiations, either Party may submit the relevant dispute to the Southern China Commission of China International
Economic and Trade Arbitration Commission for arbitration, in accordance with its Arbitration Rules. The arbitration shall be conducted
in Shenzhen, and the language used in arbitration shall be Chinese. The arbitration award shall be final and binding on all Parties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">13.3 &#22240;&#35299;&#37322;&#21644;&#23653;&#34892;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#32780;&#21457;&#29983;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#25110;&#20219;&#20309;&#20105;&#35758;&#27491;&#22312;&#36827;&#34892;&#20210;&#35009;&#26102;&#65292;&#38500;&#20105;&#35758;&#30340;&#20107;&#39033;&#22806;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21508;&#26041;&#20173;&#24212;&#32487;&#32493;&#34892;&#20351;&#21508;&#33258;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20854;&#20182;&#26435;&#21033;&#24182;&#23653;&#34892;&#21508;&#33258;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#30340;&#20854;&#20182;&#20041;&#21153;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">Upon the occurrence of any disputes arising
from the construction and performance of this Agreement or during the pending arbitration of any dispute, except for the matters under

obligations under this Agreement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>14. &#36890;&#30693;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Notices</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">14.1 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#39033;&#19979;&#35201;&#27714;&#25110;&#21457;&#20986;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#36890;&#30693;&#21644;&#20854;&#20182;&#36890;&#20449;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#19987;&#20154;&#36882;&#36865;&#12289;&#25346;&#21495;&#37038;&#23492;&#12289;&#37038;&#36164;&#39044;&#20184;&#25110;&#21830;&#19994;&#24555;&#36882;&#26381;&#21153;&#30340;&#26041;&#24335;&#21457;&#21040;&#35813;&#26041;&#19979;&#21015;&#22320;&#22336;&#12290;&#27599;&#19968;&#36890;&#30693;&#36824;&#24212;&#20877;&#20197;&#30005;&#23376;&#37038;&#20214;&#36865;&#36798;&#12290;&#35813;&#31561;&#36890;&#30693;&#35270;&#20026;&#26377;&#25928;&#36865;&#36798;&#30340;&#26085;&#26399;&#25353;&#22914;&#19979;&#26041;&#24335;&#30830;&#23450;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">All notices and other communications
required or permitted to be given pursuant to this Agreement shall be delivered personally or sent by registered mail, postage prepaid,
by a commercial courier service to the address of such party set forth below. A confirmation copy of each notice shall also be sent by
E-mail. The dates on which notices shall be deemed to have been effectively given shall be determined as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 48pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">14.2 &#36890;&#30693;&#22914;&#26524;&#26159;&#20197;&#19987;&#20154;&#36882;&#36865;&#12289;&#24555;&#36882;&#26381;&#21153;&#25110;&#25346;&#21495;&#37038;&#23492;&#12289;&#37038;&#36164;&#39044;&#20184;&#21457;&#20986;&#30340;&#65292;&#21017;&#20197;&#20110;&#35774;&#23450;&#20026;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#22320;&#22336;&#22312;&#31614;&#25910;&#25110;&#25298;&#25910;&#20043;&#26085;&#20026;&#26377;&#25928;&#36865;&#36798;&#26085;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">Notices given by personal delivery, by
courier service or by registered mail, postage prepaid, shall be deemed effectively given on the date of acceptance or refusal at the
address specified for notices.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 132pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -60pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">14.3 &#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26041;&#21464;&#26356;&#25509;&#25910;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#22320;&#22336;&#25110;&#32852;&#31995;&#20154;&#30340;&#65292;&#24212;&#25353;&#26412;&#26465;&#35268;&#23450;&#32473;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#21457;&#20986;&#36890;&#30693;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">If any Party change its address for notices
or its contact person, a notice shall be delivered to the other Parties in accordance with the terms hereof.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 48pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>15. &#20998;&#21106;&#24615;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt"><B>Severability</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&#22914;&#26524;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#26377;&#20219;&#20309;&#19968;&#26465;&#25110;&#22810;&#26465;&#35268;&#23450;&#26681;&#25454;&#20219;&#20309;&#27861;&#24459;&#25110;&#27861;&#35268;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26041;&#38754;&#34987;&#35009;&#23450;&#20026;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#65292;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20854;&#20313;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;&#26377;&#25928;&#24615;&#12289;&#21512;&#27861;&#24615;&#25110;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#24615;&#19981;&#24212;&#22240;&#27492;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#26041;&#38754;&#21463;&#21040;&#24433;&#21709;&#25110;&#25439;&#23475;&#12290;&#21508;&#26041;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#35802;&#24847;&#30923;&#21830;&#65292;&#20105;&#21462;&#20197;&#27861;&#24459;&#35768;&#21487;&#20197;&#21450;&#21508;&#26041;&#26399;&#26395;&#30340;&#26368;&#22823;&#38480;&#24230;&#20869;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#21462;&#20195;&#37027;&#20123;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#21487;&#25191;&#34892;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#32780;&#35813;&#31561;&#26377;&#25928;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#25152;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#32463;&#27982;&#25928;&#26524;&#24212;&#23613;&#21487;&#33021;&#19982;&#37027;&#20123;&#26080;&#25928;&#12289;&#19981;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#19981;&#33021;&#24378;&#21046;&#25191;&#34892;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#25152;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#32463;&#27982;&#25928;&#26524;&#30456;&#20284;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">In the event that one or several of the
provisions of this Agreement are found to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable in any aspect in accordance with any laws or regulations,
the validity, legality or enforceability of the remaining provisions of this Agreement shall not be affected or compromised in any respect.
The Parties shall strive in good faith to replace such invalid, illegal or unenforceable provisions with effective provisions that accomplish
to the greatest extent permitted by law and the intentions of the Parties, and the economic effect of such effective provisions shall
be as close as possible to the economic effect of those invalid, illegal or unenforceable provisions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">17.1 &#26412;&#21327;&#35758;&#32463;&#21508;&#26041;&#36866;&#24403;&#31614;&#32626;&#26102;&#29983;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">17.2 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20462;&#25913;&#12289;&#34917;&#20805;&#25110;&#21464;&#26356;&#65292;&#22343;&#39035;&#37319;&#29992;&#20070;&#38754;&#24418;&#24335;&#65292;&#32463;&#21508;&#26041;&#31614;&#23383;&#25110;&#30422;&#31456;&#21518;&#29983;&#25928;&#12290;</P>

to this Agreement shall be in writing and shall become effective after the affixation of the signatures or seals of the Parties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">17.3 &#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#20197;&#20013;&#25991;&#21644;&#33521;&#25991;&#20070;&#23601;&#65292;&#19968;&#24335;&#19977;&#20221;&#65292;&#36136;&#26435;&#20154;&#12289;&#20986;&#36136;&#20154;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#21508;&#25345;&#19968;&#20221;&#65292;&#20855;&#26377;&#21516;&#31561;&#25928;&#21147;&#65307;&#20013;&#33521;&#25991;&#29256;&#26412;&#22914;&#26377;&#20914;&#31361;&#65292;&#24212;&#20197;&#20013;&#25991;&#29256;&#20026;&#20934;&#12290;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 24pt; text-align: justify">This Agreement is written in Chinese
and English in three copies. Pledger, Pledgee and Party C shall hold one copy respectively. Each copy of this Agreement shall have equal
validity. In case there is any conflict between the Chinese version and the English version, the Chinese version shall prevail.</P>

&quot;Parties&quot;.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#37492;&#20110;&#65306;&#20057;&#26041;&#25345;&#26377;&#19993;&#26041;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">86.56%</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#26435;&#30410;&#12290;&#30002;&#26041;&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#31614;&#35746;&#20102;&#21672;&#35810;&#19982;&#26381;&#21153;&#21327;&#35758;&#12289;&#19994;&#21153;&#21512;&#20316;&#21512;&#21516;&#31561;&#19968;&#31995;&#21015;&#25511;&#21046;&#24615;&#21327;&#35758;&#65288;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25511;&#21046;&#21327;&#35758;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65289;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Whereas: Party B holds 86.58%
of the equity interest in Party C. Party A and Party C have executed a Consultation and Service Agreement, Business Cooperation Agreement
and other control agreements (the &ldquo;Control Agreements&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt SimSun; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&#29616;&#21508;&#26041;&#21327;&#21830;&#19968;&#33268;&#65292;&#36798;&#25104;&#22914;&#19979;&#21327;&#35758;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Now therefore, upon mutual
discussion and negotiation, the Parties have reached the following agreement:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>1.</B></FONT><B>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;&#20080;&#21334;</FONT></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21pt"><B>Sale and Purchase
of Equity Interest</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.1</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25480;&#20104;&#26435;&#21033;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Option Granted</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#37492;&#20110;&#30002;&#26041;&#21521;&#20057;&#26041;&#25903;&#20184;&#20102;&#20154;&#27665;&#24065;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20803;&#20316;&#20026;&#23545;&#20215;&#65292;&#19988;&#20057;&#26041;&#30830;&#35748;&#25910;&#21040;&#24182;&#35748;&#20026;&#35813;&#23545;&#20215;&#36275;&#22815;&#65292;&#20057;&#26041;&#22312;&#27492;&#19981;&#21487;&#25764;&#38144;&#22320;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#22312;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#20801;&#35768;&#30340;&#21069;&#25552;&#19979;&#65292;&#30002;&#26041;&#21487;&#20197;&#25353;&#29031;&#33258;&#34892;&#20915;&#23450;&#30340;&#34892;&#20351;&#27493;&#39588;&#65292;&#24182;&#25353;&#29031;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31532;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.3</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26465;&#25152;&#36848;&#30340;&#20215;&#26684;&#65292;&#35201;&#27714;&#20057;&#26041;&#23653;&#34892;&#21644;&#23436;&#25104;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#35201;&#27714;&#30340;&#19968;&#20999;&#23457;&#25209;&#21644;&#30331;&#35760;&#25163;&#32493;&#65292;&#20351;&#24471;&#30002;&#26041;&#21487;&#20197;&#38543;&#26102;&#19968;&#27425;&#25110;&#22810;&#27425;&#20174;&#20057;&#26041;&#36141;&#20080;&#65292;&#25110;&#25351;&#23450;&#19968;&#20154;&#25110;&#22810;&#20154;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20174;&#20057;&#26041;&#36141;&#20080;&#20057;&#26041;&#25152;&#25345;&#26377;&#30340;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#19981;&#36229;&#36807;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">86.58%</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;(&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#12290;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#35813;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#20026;&#29420;&#23478;&#30340;&#12290;&#38500;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#22806;&#65292;&#20219;&#20309;&#31532;&#19977;&#20154;&#22343;&#19981;&#24471;&#20139;&#26377;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#25110;&#20854;&#20182;&#19982;&#20057;&#26041;&#32929;&#26435;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#26435;&#21033;&#12290;&#19993;&#26041;&#29305;&#27492;&#21516;&#24847;&#20057;&#26041;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#25480;&#20104;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#12290;&#26412;&#27454;&#21450;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#25152;&#35268;&#23450;&#30340;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20154;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25351;&#20010;&#20154;&#12289;&#20844;&#21496;&#12289;&#21512;&#33829;&#20225;&#19994;&#12289;&#21512;&#20249;&#12289;&#20225;&#19994;&#12289;&#20449;&#25176;&#25110;&#38750;&#20844;&#21496;&#32452;&#32455;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">In consideration of the payment
of RMB 1 by Party A, the receipt and adequacy of which is hereby acknowledged by Party B, Party B hereby irrevocably agrees that, on the
condition that it is permitted by the PRC laws, Party A has the right to require Party B to fulfill and complete all approval and registration
procedures required under PRC laws for Party A to purchase, or designate one or more persons (each, a &quot;Designee&quot;) to purchase,
Party up to 86.58% of B&rsquo;s equity interests in Party C, once or at multiple times at any time in part or in whole at Party A's sole
and absolute discretion and at the price described in Section 1.3 herein (such right being the &quot;Equity Interest Purchase Option&quot;).
Party A&rsquo;s Equity Interest Purchase Option shall be exclusive. Except for Party A and the Designee(s), no other person shall be entitled
to the Equity Interest Purchase Option or other rights with respect to the equity interests of Party B. Party C hereby agrees to the grant
by Party B of the Equity Interest Purchase Option to Party A. The term &quot;person&quot; as used herein shall refer to individuals, corporations,
partnerships, partners, enterprises, trusts or non-corporate organizations.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.2</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34892;&#20351;&#27493;&#39588;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Steps for Exercise of Equity
Interest Purchase Option</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 45pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#30002;&#26041;&#34892;&#20351;&#20854;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#20197;&#31526;&#21512;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#21644;&#27861;&#35268;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#20026;&#21069;&#25552;&#12290;&#30002;&#26041;&#34892;&#20351;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#26102;&#65292;&#24212;&#21521;&#20057;&#26041;&#21457;&#20986;&#20070;&#38754;&#36890;&#30693;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#36890;&#30693;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65292;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#36890;&#30693;&#24212;&#36733;&#26126;&#20197;&#19979;&#20107;&#39033;&#65306;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(a)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#30002;&#26041;&#20851;&#20110;&#34892;&#20351;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#30340;&#20915;&#23450;&#65307;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(b)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#30002;&#26041;&#25311;&#20174;&#20057;&#26041;&#36141;&#20080;&#30340;&#32929;&#26435;&#20221;&#39069;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;)&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65307;&#21644;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(c)&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#36141;&#20080;&#26085;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">/</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#36716;&#35753;&#26085;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Subject to the provisions
of the laws and regulations of China, Party A may exercise the Equity Interest Purchase Option by issuing a written notice to Party B
(the &quot;Equity Interest Purchase Option Notice&quot;), specifying: (a) Party A's decision to exercise the Equity Interest Purchase
Option; (b) the portion of equity interests to be purchased from Party B (the &quot;Optioned Interests&quot;); and (c) the date for purchasing
the Optioned Interests and/or the date for transfer of the Optioned Interests.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>

    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.3</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;&#20080;&#20215;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Equity Interest Purchase
Price</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#20080;&#20215;&#65288;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#22522;&#20934;&#20080;&#20215;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65289;&#24212;&#20026;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#25152;&#20801;&#35768;&#30340;&#26368;&#20302;&#20215;&#26684;&#12290;&#22914;&#26524;&#22312;&#30002;&#26041;&#34892;&#26435;&#26102;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#35201;&#27714;&#35780;&#20272;&#32929;&#26435;&#65292;&#21508;&#26041;&#36890;&#36807;&#35802;&#20449;&#21407;&#21017;&#21478;&#34892;&#21830;&#23450;&#65292;&#24182;&#22312;&#35780;&#20272;&#22522;&#30784;&#19978;&#23545;&#35813;&#32929;&#26435;&#20080;&#20215;&#36827;&#34892;&#24517;&#35201;&#35843;&#25972;&#65292;&#20197;&#31526;&#21512;&#24403;&#26102;&#36866;&#29992;&#20043;&#20219;&#20309;&#20013;&#22269;&#27861;&#24459;&#20043;&#35201;&#27714;&#65288;&#32479;&#31216;&#65292;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&ldquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#32929;&#26435;&#20080;&#20215;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&rdquo;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65289;&#12290;&#22914;&#26524;&#24403;&#22522;&#20934;&#20080;&#20215;&#39640;&#20110;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#27880;&#20876;&#36164;&#26412;&#26102;&#65288;&#33509;&#38750;&#36141;&#20080;&#20840;&#37096;&#32929;&#26435;&#26102;&#65292;&#25353;&#27604;&#20363;&#35745;&#31639;&#65289;&#65292;&#20057;&#26041;&#24212;&#25353;&#29031;&#30002;&#26041;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#26041;&#24335;&#23558;&#39640;&#20986;&#37096;&#20998;&#36820;&#36824;&#32473;&#30002;&#26041;&#25110;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20154;&#22763;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">The purchase price of the
Optioned Interests (the &quot;Base Price&quot;) shall be the lowest price allowed by the laws of China. If appraisal is required by the
laws of China at the time when Party A exercises the Equity Interest Purchase Option, the Parties shall negotiate in good faith and based
on the appraisal result make necessary adjustment to the Equity Interest Purchase Price so that it complies with any and all then applicable
laws of China (collectively, the &quot;Equity Interest Purchase Price&quot;). When the price is higher than the registered capital of
Party C, calculated pro rata for purchase of less than all of the Equity Interest, the excessive part of the price shall be returned to
Party A or its designee in a manner as instructed by Party A.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.4</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#36716;&#35753;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Transfer of Optioned Interests</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt SimSun; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&#30002;&#26041;&#27599;&#27425;&#34892;&#20351;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#26102;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">For each exercise of the
Equity Interest Purchase Option:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.55pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.4.1</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20057;&#26041;&#24212;&#36131;&#25104;&#19993;&#26041;&#21450;&#26102;&#21484;&#24320;&#32929;&#19996;&#20250;&#20250;&#35758;&#65292;&#22312;&#35813;&#20250;&#35758;&#19978;&#65292;&#24212;&#36890;&#36807;&#25209;&#20934;&#20057;&#26041;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">/</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25110;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#36716;&#35753;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#30340;&#20915;&#35758;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Party B shall cause Party
C to promptly convene a shareholders&rsquo; meeting, at which a resolution shall be adopted approving Party B's transfer of the Optioned
Interests to Party A and/or the Designee(s);</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.4.2</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20057;&#26041;&#24212;&#23601;&#20854;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">/</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25110;&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#36716;&#35753;&#34987;&#36141;&#20080;&#32929;&#26435;&#21462;&#24471;&#19993;&#26041;&#20854;&#20182;&#32929;&#19996;&#21516;&#24847;&#35813;&#36716;&#35753;&#24182;&#25918;&#24323;&#20248;&#20808;&#36141;&#20080;&#26435;&#30340;&#20070;&#38754;&#22768;&#26126;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Party B shall obtain written
statements from the other shareholders of Party C giving consent to the transfer of the equity interest to Party A and/or the Designee(s)
and waiving any right of first refusal related thereto.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 84pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 84pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->3<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt"></P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 84pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.4.3</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20057;&#26041;&#24212;&#19982;&#30002;&#26041;&#21644;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">/</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25110;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;(</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#22312;&#36866;&#29992;&#30340;&#24773;&#20917;&#19979;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#34987;&#25351;&#23450;&#20154;&#25353;&#29031;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#21450;&#32929;&#26435;&#36141;&#20080;&#36890;&#30693;&#30340;&#35268;&#23450;&#65292;&#20026;&#27599;&#27425;&#36716;&#35753;&#31614;&#35746;&#32929;&#26435;&#36716;&#35753;&#21512;&#21516;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Party B shall execute a share
transfer contract with respect to each transfer with Party A and/or each Designee (whichever is applicable), in accordance with the provisions
of this Agreement and the Equity Interest Purchase Option Notice regarding the Optioned Interests;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">1.4.4&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: <P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">The relevant Parties shall
execute all other necessary contracts, agreements or documents, obtain all necessary government licenses and permits and take all necessary
actions to transfer valid ownership of the Optioned Interests to Party A and/or the Designee(s), unencumbered by any security interests,
and cause Party A and/or the Designee(s) to become the registered owner(s) of the Optioned Interests. For the purpose of this Section
and this Agreement, &quot;security interests&quot; shall include securities, mortgages, third party's rights or interests, any stock options,
acquisition right, right of first refusal, right to offset, ownership retention or other security arrangements, but shall be deemed to
exclude any security interest created by this Agreement and Party B's Equity Pledge Agreement. &quot;Party B's Equity Pledge Agreement&quot;
as used in this Section and this Agreement shall refer to the Equity Pledge Agreement (&quot;Party B's Equity Pledge Agreement&quot;)
executed by and among Party A, Party B and Party C as of the date hereof, whereby Party B pledges all of its equity interests in Party
C to Party A, in order to guarantee Party C's performance of its obligations under the Control Agreements executed by and between Party
C and Party A.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><B>2.</B></FONT><B>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25215;&#35834;</FONT></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 24.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26377;&#20851;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#25215;&#35834;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Covenants regarding Party
C</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.2pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 28.45pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt SimSun; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">&#20057;&#26041;&#65288;&#20316;&#20026;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#32929;&#19996;&#65289;&#21644;&#19993;&#26041;&#22312;&#27492;&#25215;&#35834;&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 19.05pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 30.6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Party B (as the shareholders
of Party C) and Party C hereby covenant as follows:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.65pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 49.65pt; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.1&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#24418;&#24335;&#34917;&#20805;&#12289;&#26356;&#25913;&#25110;&#20462;&#25913;&#19993;&#26041;&#20844;&#21496;&#31456;&#31243;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#22686;&#21152;&#25110;&#20943;&#23569;&#20854;&#27880;&#20876;&#36164;&#26412;&#65292;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#25913;&#21464;&#20854;&#27880;&#20876;&#36164;&#26412;&#32467;&#26500;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not in any manner supplement, change or amend the articles of association and bylaws of Party C, increase
or decrease its registered capital, or change its structure of registered capital in other manners;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.2</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#25353;&#29031;&#33391;&#22909;&#30340;&#36130;&#21153;&#21644;&#21830;&#19994;&#26631;&#20934;&#21450;&#24815;&#20363;&#65292;&#20445;&#25345;&#20854;&#20844;&#21496;&#30340;&#23384;&#32493;&#65292;&#23457;&#24910;&#22320;&#21450;&#26377;&#25928;&#22320;&#32463;&#33829;&#20854;&#19994;&#21153;&#21644;&#22788;&#29702;&#20107;&#21153;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">They shall maintain Party
C's corporate existence in accordance with good financial and business standards and practices by prudently and effectively operating
its business and handling its affairs;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.3&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#22312;&#26412;&#21512;&#21516;&#31614;&#32626;&#20043;&#26085;&#36215;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#26102;&#38388;&#20986;&#21806;&#12289;&#36716;&#35753;&#12289;&#25269;&#25276;&#25110;&#20197;&#20854;&#20182;&#26041;&#24335;&#22788;&#32622;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#36164;&#20135;&#12289;&#19994;&#21153;&#25110;&#25910;&#20837;&#30340;&#21512;&#27861;&#25110;&#21463;&#30410;&#26435;&#30410;&#65292;&#25110;&#20801;&#35768;&#22312;&#20854;&#19978;&#35774;&#32622;&#20219;&#20309;&#20854;&#20182;&#25285;&#20445;&#26435;&#30410;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not at any time following the date hereof, sell, transfer, mortgage or dispose of in any manner any assets
of Party C or legal or beneficial interest in the business or revenues of Party C, or allow the encumbrance thereon of any security interest;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.4&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#21457;&#29983;&#12289;&#32487;&#25215;&#12289;&#20445;&#35777;&#25110;&#23481;&#35768;&#23384;&#22312;&#20219;&#20309;&#20538;&#21153;&#65292;&#20294;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(i)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#27491;&#24120;&#25110;&#26085;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#20135;&#29983;&#32780;&#19981;&#26159;&#36890;&#36807;&#20511;&#27454;&#26041;&#24335;&#20135;&#29983;&#30340;&#20538;&#21153;&#65307;&#21644;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(ii)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#24050;&#21521;&#30002;&#26041;&#25259;&#38706;&#21644;&#24471;&#21040;&#30002;&#26041;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#30340;&#20538;&#21153;&#38500;&#22806;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not incur, inherit, guarantee or suffer the existence of any debt, except for (i) debts incurred in the
ordinary course of business other than through loans; and (ii) debts disclosed to Party A for which Party A's written consent has been
obtained;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.5&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#19968;&#30452;&#22312;&#27491;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#32463;&#33829;&#25152;&#26377;&#19994;&#21153;&#65292;&#20197;&#20445;&#25345;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#36164;&#20135;&#20215;&#20540;&#65292;&#19981;&#36827;&#34892;&#20219;&#20309;&#36275;&#20197;&#24433;&#21709;&#20854;&#32463;&#33829;&#29366;&#20917;&#21644;&#36164;&#20135;&#20215;&#20540;&#30340;&#20316;&#20026;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">/</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#19981;&#20316;&#20026;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">They shall always operate
all of Party C's businesses during the ordinary course of business to maintain the asset value of Party C and refrain from any action/omission
that may affect Party C's operating status and asset value;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.6&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#35753;&#19993;&#26041;&#31614;&#35746;&#20219;&#20309;&#37325;&#22823;&#21512;&#21516;&#65292;&#20294;&#22312;&#27491;&#24120;&#19994;&#21153;&#36807;&#31243;&#20013;&#31614;&#35746;&#30340;&#21512;&#21516;&#38500;&#22806;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#23601;&#26412;&#27573;&#32780;&#35328;&#65292;&#22914;&#26524;&#19968;&#20221;&#21512;&#21516;&#30340;&#24635;&#37329;&#39069;&#36229;&#36807;&#20154;&#27665;&#24065;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">100,000</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20803;&#65292;&#21363;&#34987;&#35270;&#20026;&#37325;&#22823;&#21512;&#21516;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">)</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause Party C to execute any major contract, except the contracts in the ordinary course of business
(for purpose of this subsection, a contract with a price exceeding RMB 100,000 shall be deemed a major contract);</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.7</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#19981;&#24471;&#21521;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#25552;&#20379;&#36151;&#27454;&#25110;&#20449;&#36151;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause Party C to provide any person with any loan or credit;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->5<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Equity Option Agreement</P></DIV>

    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.8</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#24212;&#30002;&#26041;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#21521;&#20854;&#25552;&#20379;&#25152;&#26377;&#20851;&#20110;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33829;&#36816;&#21644;&#36130;&#21153;&#29366;&#20917;&#30340;&#36164;&#26009;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">They shall provide Party
A with information on Party C's business operations and financial condition at Party A's request;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.9&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#22914;&#30002;&#26041;&#25552;&#20986;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#24212;&#20174;&#30002;&#26041;&#25509;&#21463;&#30340;&#20445;&#38505;&#20844;&#21496;&#22788;&#36141;&#20080;&#21644;&#25345;&#26377;&#26377;&#20851;&#20854;&#36164;&#20135;&#21644;&#19994;&#21153;&#30340;&#20445;&#38505;&#65292;&#35813;&#20445;&#38505;&#30340;&#37329;&#39069;&#21644;&#38505;&#31181;&#24212;&#19982;&#32463;&#33829;&#31867;&#20284;&#19994;&#21153;&#30340;&#20844;&#21496;&#19968;&#33268;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">If requested by Party A,
they shall procure and maintain insurance in respect of Party C's assets and business from an insurance carrier acceptable to Party A,
at an amount and type of coverage typical for companies that operate similar businesses;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.10</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#19981;&#24471;&#19982;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#21512;&#24182;&#25110;&#32852;&#21512;&#65292;&#25110;&#23545;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#36827;&#34892;&#25910;&#36141;&#25110;&#25237;&#36164;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall not cause or permit Party C to merge, consolidate with, acquire or invest in any person;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.11</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#23558;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#25110;&#21487;&#33021;&#21457;&#29983;&#30340;&#19982;&#19993;&#26041;&#36164;&#20135;&#12289;&#19994;&#21153;&#25110;&#25910;&#20837;&#26377;&#20851;&#30340;&#35785;&#35772;&#12289;&#20210;&#35009;&#25110;&#34892;&#25919;&#31243;&#24207;&#31435;&#21363;&#36890;&#30693;&#30002;&#26041;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 21.15pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.1pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">They shall immediately notify
Party A of the occurrence or possible occurrence of any litigation, arbitration or administrative proceedings relating to Party C's assets,
business or revenue;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.12&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#20026;&#20445;&#25345;&#19993;&#26041;&#23545;&#20854;&#20840;&#37096;&#36164;&#20135;&#30340;&#25152;&#26377;&#26435;&#65292;&#31614;&#32626;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25991;&#20214;&#65292;&#37319;&#21462;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#34892;&#21160;&#21644;&#25552;&#20986;&#25152;&#26377;&#24517;&#35201;&#25110;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25511;&#21578;&#25110;&#23545;&#25152;&#26377;&#32034;&#20607;&#36827;&#34892;&#24517;&#35201;&#21644;&#36866;&#24403;&#30340;&#25239;&#36777;&#65307;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">To maintain the ownership
by Party C of all of its assets, they shall execute all necessary or appropriate documents, take all necessary or appropriate actions
and file all necessary or appropriate complaints or raise necessary and appropriate defenses against all claims;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.13&nbsp;</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#20197;&#20219;&#20309;&#24418;&#24335;&#27966;&#21457;&#32929;&#24687;&#20104;&#21508;&#32929;&#19996;&#65292;&#20294;&#19968;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#19993;&#26041;&#24212;&#31435;&#21363;&#23558;&#20854;&#25152;&#26377;&#21487;&#20998;&#37197;&#21033;&#28070;&#20840;&#37096;&#31435;&#21363;&#20998;&#37197;&#32473;&#20854;&#21508;&#32929;&#19996;&#65307;&#21450;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">Without the prior written
consent of Party A, they shall ensure that Party C shall not in any manner distribute dividends to its shareholders, provided that upon
Party A's written request, Party C shall immediately distribute all distributable profits to its shareholders; and</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">2.1.14</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="font-family: SimSun">&#26681;&#25454;&#30002;&#26041;&#30340;&#35201;&#27714;&#65292;&#22996;&#20219;&#30001;&#20854;&#25351;&#23450;&#30340;&#20219;&#20309;&#20154;&#22763;&#20986;&#20219;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#65307;&#26410;&#32463;&#30002;&#26041;&#20107;&#20808;&#20070;&#38754;&#21516;&#24847;&#65292;&#19981;&#24471;&#26356;&#25442;&#19993;&#26041;&#30340;&#33891;&#20107;&#12290;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 21.3pt">At the request of Party A,
they shall appoint any persons designated by Party A as directors of Party C; without the prior written consent of Party A, they shall
not replace the directors of Party C.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 85.05pt; text-align: justify"></P>
